251\t\n   252\tdef _video_profile(prompt: str, quality_profile: str) ->

_build_mesh_obj(prompt: str, quality_profile: str, mesh_kind: str) ->

_build_cube_obj(prompt: str) -> tuple[str, int, int]:\n   287\t    comment = 
prompt.replace("\\n", " ").replace("\\r", " ")\n   288\t    text = (\n   289\t 
f"# Generated by Jarvis local 3D adapter\\n# prompt: {comment}\\n"\n   290\t   
"o jarvis_cube\\n"\n   291\t        "v -0.5 -0.5 -0.5\\n"\n   292\t        "v

text, 8, 6\n   307\t\n   308\t\n   309\tdef _build_sphere_obj(prompt: str, 
rings: int, segments: int) -> tuple[str, int, int]:\n   310\t    comment = 
prompt.replace("\\n", " ").replace("\\r", " ")\n   311\t    vertices: 
list[tuple[float, float, float]] = []\n   312\t    faces: list[tuple[int, int, 
int]] = []\n   313\t\n   314\t    # Top pole.\n   315\t    
vertices.append((0.0, 0.5, 0.0))\n   316\t\n   317\t    # Intermediate rings.\n
318\t    for ring in range(1, rings):\n   319\t        theta = math.pi * ring /
rings\n   320\t        y = 0.5 * math.cos(theta)\n   321\t        radius = 0.5 
* math.sin(theta)\n   322\t        for seg in range(segments):\n   323\t       
phi = 2.0 * math.pi * seg / segments\n   324\t            x = radius * 
math.cos(phi)\n   325\t            z = radius * math.sin(phi)\n   326\t        
vertices.append((x, y, z))\n   327\t\n   328\t    # Bottom pole.\n   329\t    
vertices.append((0.0, -0.5, 0.0))\n   330\t    top_index = 1\n   331\t    
first_ring = 2\n   332\t    last_ring = first_ring + (rings - 2) * segments\n  
333\t    bottom_index = len(vertices)\n   334\t\n   335\t    # Top fan.\n   
336\t    for seg in range(segments):\n   337\t        a = top_index\n   338\t  
b = first_ring + seg\n   339\t        c = first_ring + ((seg + 1) % segments)\n
340\t        faces.append((a, b, c))\n   341\t\n   342\t    # Middle strips.\n 
343\t    for ring in range(rings - 2):\n   344\t        curr = first_ring + 
ring * segments\n   345\t        nxt = curr + segments\n   346\t        for seg
in range(segments):\n   347\t            a = curr + seg\n   348\t            b 
= curr + ((seg + 1) % segments)\n   349\t            c = nxt + ((seg + 1) % 
segments)\n   350\t            d = nxt + seg\n   351\t            
faces.append((a, d, c))\n   352\t            faces.append((a, c, b))\n   
353\t\n   354\t    # Bottom fan.\n   355\t    for seg in range(segments):\n   
356\t        a = bottom_index\n   357\t        b = last_ring + ((seg + 1) % 
segments)\n   358\t        c = last_ring + seg\n   359\t        
faces.append((a, b, c))\n   360\t\n   361\t    lines = [f"# Generated by Jarvis

lines.extend([f"v {x:.6f} {y:.6f} {z:.6f}" for x, y, z in vertices])\n   363\t 
lines.extend([f"f {a} {b} {c}" for a, b, c in faces])\n   364\t    return 
"\\n".join(lines) + "\\n", len(vertices), len(faces)\n   365\t\n   366\t\n   
367\tdef _build_cylinder_obj(prompt: str, segments: int) -> tuple[str, int, 
int]:\n   368\t    comment = prompt.replace("\\n", " ").replace("\\r", " ")\n  
369\t    vertices: list[tuple[float, float, float]] = []\n   370\t    faces:

vertices.append((0.0, 0.5, 0.0))\n   374\t    vertices.append((0.0, -0.5, 
0.0))\n   375\t    top_center = 1\n   376\t    bottom_center = 2\n   377\t\n   
378\t    top_ring_start = 3\n   379\t    for seg in range(segments):\n   380\t 
angle = 2.0 * math.pi * seg / segments\n   381\t        x = 0.5 * 
math.cos(angle)\n   382\t        z = 0.5 * math.sin(angle)\n   383\t        
vertices.append((x, 0.5, z))\n   384\t        vertices.append((x, -0.5, z))\n  
385\t\n   386\t    # Top and bottom caps.\n   387\t    for seg in 
range(segments):\n   388\t        top_a = top_ring_start + (seg * 2)\n   389\t 
top_b = top_ring_start + (((seg + 1) % segments) * 2)\n   390\t        bottom_a
= top_a + 1\n   391\t        bottom_b = top_b + 1\n   392\t        
faces.append((top_center, top_a, top_b))\n   393\t        
faces.append((bottom_center, bottom_b, bottom_a))\n   394\t\n   395\t        # 
Side quads as triangles.\n   396\t        faces.append((top_a, bottom_a, 
bottom_b))\n   397\t        faces.append((top_a, bottom_b, top_b))\n   398\t\n 
399\t    lines = [f"# Generated by Jarvis local 3D adapter", f"# prompt: 
{comment}", "o jarvis_cylinder"]\n   400\t    lines.extend([f"v {x:.6f} {y:.6f}
{z:.6f}" for x, y, z in vertices])\n   401\t    lines.extend([f"f {a} {b} {c}" 
for a, b, c in faces])\n   402\t    return "\\n".join(lines) + "\\n", 
len(vertices), len(faces)\n',

_write_tone(path: Path, freq: float, *, duration_s: float = 1.6, rate: int =

base + 0.03 * np.sin((2.0 * np.pi * (freq * 2.0) * t) + (phase / 3.0))\n    
16\t    signal += 0.01 * np.random.default_rng(42).normal(size=signal.shape)\n

"wb") as wf:\n    21\t        wf.setnchannels(1)\n    22\t        
wf.setsampwidth(2)\n    23\t        wf.setframerate(rate)\n    24\t        
wf.writeframes(pcm.tobytes())\n    25\t\n    26\t\n    27\tdef

_write_tone(diff, 720.0, phase=0.0)\n    34\t\n    35\t    enrolled =

threshold=0.0)\n    40\t    assert same_score.score > diff_score.score\n
